## **190. Post by `@coryd.dev` on 2026-07-07**

<div class="bsky-card" markdown="1">

<div class="bsky-header" markdown="1">

<img src="https://cdn.bsky.app/img/avatar/plain/did:plc:sttgf52vkk46f6yuknvqxvgh/bafkreibcmy5qz6bq64oq2awoi66f6u5qcshdq7jqlxonyjlb3ilc6udaee" class="bsky-avatar">

<div class="bsky-content" markdown="1">

🔗 Publishing on the Atmosphere with Standard.site via @vale.rocks tech atproto bluesky Standard.site provides a set of lexicons for publishing long-form content on the internet using the same https://piccalil.li/blog/publishing-on-the-atmosphere-with-standardsite/?ref=main-rss-feed







<a href="https://piccalil.li/blog/publishing-on-the-atmosphere-with-standardsite/?ref=main-rss-feed" class="bsky-link-preview-wrapper" target="_blank">
<div class="bsky-link-preview" markdown="1">

<div class="link-info" markdown="1">
